Music Blocks Project - My Project

No description provided

This project was created in Music Blocks (https://musicblocks.sugarlabs.org). Music Blocks is a collection of tools for exploring fundamental musical concepts in a fun way. Music Blocks is a Free/Libre Software application. The source code can be accessed at https://github.com/sugarlabs/musicblocks. For more information, please consult the Music Blocks Guide.

To run this project, open Music Blocks in a web browser and drag and drop this file into the browser window. Alternatively, open the file in Music Blocks using the Load project button.
